***samoerai.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:samoerai.html>samoerai</a> (15621)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Japanese language">Japanese</a></span> <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">侍</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-tr tr">さむらい, samurai</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:samoerai.html>samoerai</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:samoerai.html>samoerai</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">samoerais</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:samoerai.html>samoeraitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***sanctie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sanctie.html>sanctie</a> (59328)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">sanction</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sānctiō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sanctie.html>sanctie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sancties.html>sancties</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sanctie.html>sanctietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly diplomacy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sanction <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">measure intended to encourage compliance</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

***sanctus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sanctus.html>sanctus</a> (100221)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>Perfect</a> passive participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sanciō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">consecrate, appoint as sacred</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="la">sānctus</strong> (<i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">sāncta</b>, <i>neuter</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">sānctum</b>, <i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">sānctior</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">sānctissimus</b>); <i>first/second-declension participle</i>
</p>
<ol><li>sacred, made inviolable, having <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> established as sacred.</li>
<li>venerable, august, divine, blessed, holy, saintly
<ul><li>4th century, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/St_Jerome" class="extiw" title="w:St Jerome">St Jerome</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgate" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgate">Vulgate</a>, Tobit 3:25
<dl><dd>et missus est angelus Domini <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sanctus.html>sanctus</a></b> Rafahel ut curaret ambos quorum <a href = vnd.unilang:uno.html>uno</a> tempore fuerat oratio in conspectu Domini recitata (And the <b>holy</b> angel of the Lord, Raphael <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> sent to heal them both, whose prayers at one time <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> rehearsed in the sight of the Lord.)</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="la">sānctus</strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">sānctī</b>); <i>second declension</i>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A saint; person who <a href = vnd.unilang:lives.html>lives</a> a holy and virtuous life.
<dl><dd>"Dorothy Day erat sancta viva." (Dorothy Day <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a living saint.)</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> officially proclaimed as having lived a life of heroic virtue.
<dl><dd>"Kateri Tekakwitha sancta proclamata est." (Kateri Tekakwitha <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> proclaimed a saint.)</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A title given to (2), usually capitalized, prefixed to the person's name.
<dl><dd>"<a href = vnd.unilang:sanctus.html>Sanctus</a> Stephanus Protomartyr"</dd></dl></li></ol>

***sander.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sander.html>sander</a> (73085)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sand</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sander.html>sander</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">sanders</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person employed to sand wood.</li>
<li>A machine to mechanize the process of sanding.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">railway</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A device which spreads sand on the <a href = vnd.unilang:rails.html>rails</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a>, snowy or icy conditions to improve traction.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A small device resembling a salt shaker but containing sand that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:shaken.html>shaken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> a document to remove excess ink.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">sandi</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">sondy</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">sandiȝ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">sandiġ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:sandy.html>sandy</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sand</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">zandig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:sandy.html>sandy</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">sandig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:sandy.html>sandy</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">sandig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:sandy.html>sandy</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li>Covered with sand.</li>
<li>Sprinkled with sand.</li>
<li>Containing sand.

<li>Like sand, especially in texture.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1898</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Winston_Churchill_(novelist)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Winston Churchill (novelist)">Winston Churchill</a>,  chapter 4, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Celebrity" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Celebrity">The Celebrity</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. So roundly <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> he vituperate the inn management in particular, and with such a loud flow of <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a>, that I trembled lest he should be <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> on the <a href = vnd.unilang:veranda.html>veranda</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>

***sant.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sant.html>sant</a> (29674)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*samdaz</i>, whence also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">sand</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:sant.html>sant</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">sand</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">sandr</i>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sámh₂dʰos</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sarcofaag.html>sarcofaag</a> (21803)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">sarcophage</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sarcophagus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σαρκοφάγος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sarkophágos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">coffin of limestone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, <span class="ann-pos">noun</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, so named from a supposed property of consuming the flesh of corpses laid in it, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σαρκοφάγος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sarkophágos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flesh-eating, carnivorous</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from genitive <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σαρκός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sarkós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> of <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σάρξ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sárx</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flesh, meat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">-φάγος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-phágos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἔφαγον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">éphagon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, past of <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">φαγεῖν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">phageîn</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to eat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>)
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sarcofaag.html>sarcofaag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sarcofagen.html>sarcofagen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sarcofaag.html>sarcofaagje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">sarcophagus</span></li></ol>

***sat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sat.html>sat</a> (20235)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:sat.html>sat</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sadaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">satt</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zat</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="lb"><a href = vnd.unilang:sat.html>sat</a></strong> (<i>masculine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lb">saten</b>, <i>neuter</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lb"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:sat.html>sat</a></strong></b>, <i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lb">méi <a href = vnd.unilang:sat.html>sat</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lb">am saatsten</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>full, sated
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="lb"><a href = vnd.unilang:ech.html>Ech</a> sinn esou <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sat.html>sat</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm so <b>full</b>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>drunk, inebriated</li></ol>
</body>

***satchel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:satchel.html>satchel</a> (88490)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First recorded circa 1340, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:sachel.html>sachel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">saccellum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">money bag, purse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a diminutive of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sacculus</i>, itself a diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">saccus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bag</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sack</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:satchel.html>satchel</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">satchels</b>)
</p>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/satchel_(bag)" class="extiw" title="w:satchel (bag)"><a href = vnd.unilang:satchel.html>satchel</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/satchel_(bag)" class="extiw" title="w:satchel (bag)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<ol><li>A bag or case with one or two shoulder straps, especially used to carry books etc.
<ul><li><i>"Come, now, take yourselves off, like good boys and <a href = vnd.unilang:girls.html>girls</a>," he <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a>; and the whole assemblage, dark and light, disappeared through a <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> into a large verandah, followed by <a href = vnd.unilang:eva.html>Eva</a>, who carried a large <b><a href = vnd.unilang:satchel.html>satchel</a></b>, which she <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> filling with apples, <a href = vnd.unilang:nuts.html>nuts</a>, candy, ribbons, laces, and toys of every description, during her whole homeward journey.</i></li></ul></li></ol>

***satelliet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:satelliet.html>satelliet</a> (4337)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">satellite</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">satelles</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:satelliet.html>satelliet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:satellieten.html>satellieten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:satelliet.html>satellietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>satellite (natural: e.g. Phobos and Deimos)</li>
<li>satellite (artificial: e.g. Sputnik)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">natural satellite</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maan.html>maan</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">artificial satellite</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">kunstmaan</span></li></ul>
